<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="background:transparent; width:100%;">
<tbody><tr>
<td style="width:50%; text-align:left;"><b><a href="/wiki/Speaker_of_the_United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="Speaker of the United States House of Representatives">Speaker</a> before election</b><br />
<p><a href="/wiki/Dennis_Hastert" title="Dennis Hastert">Dennis Hastert</a><br />
<a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(US)" class="mw-redirect" title="Republican Party (US)">Republican</a>
</p>
</td>
<td style="width:50%; text-align:right;"><b>Elected <a href="/wiki/Speaker_of_the_United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="Speaker of the United States House of Representatives">Speaker</a></b> <br />
<p><a href="/wiki/Dennis_Hastert" title="Dennis Hastert">Dennis Hastert</a><br />
<a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(US)" class="mw-redirect" title="Republican Party (US)">Republican</a>
</p>
</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>2002 United States House of Representatives elections</b> were held on 5 November 2002, in the middle of <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a>'s first term. Although it was a <a href="/wiki/Midterm_election" title="Midterm election">midterm election</a> under a Republican president, the Republican Party gained a net eight seats, solidifying their majority. Some speculate that this may have been due to increased support for the President's party in the wake of the <a href="/wiki/September_11_attacks" title="September 11 attacks">September 11 attacks</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This was one of two mid-term elections in which the party of the incumbent President increased their number of seats in both the House and the Senate (the other such mid-term elections were in <a href="/wiki/1934_United_States_elections" title="1934 United States elections">1934</a>). It was the sixth midterm election in which the President's party increased its number of seats in the House, after <a href="/wiki/1814_and_1815_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections" title="1814 and 1815 United States House of Representatives elections">1814</a>, <a href="/wiki/1822_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections" class="mw-redirect" title="1822 United States House of Representatives elections">1822</a>, <a href="/wiki/1902_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections" title="1902 United States House of Representatives elections">1902</a>, <a href="/wiki/1934_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections" title="1934 United States House of Representatives elections">1934</a>, and <a href="/wiki/1998_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections" title="1998 United States House of Representatives elections">1998</a>), and is the only midterm election since <a href="/wiki/1978_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections" title="1978 United States House of Representatives elections">1978</a> which left the President's party in control of the House.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Special_elections">Special elections</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2002_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Special elections">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_special_elections_to_the_United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="List of special elections to the United States House of Representatives">List of special elections to the United States House of Representatives</a></div>
<p>Two special elections were held for members to serve the remainder of the term ending January 3, 2003.

<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2002_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections_in_Georgia" title="2002 United States House of Representatives elections in Georgia">2002 United States House of Representatives elections in Georgia</a></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Indiana">Indiana</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2002_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Indiana">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2002_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections_in_Indiana" title="2002 United States House of Representatives elections in Indiana">2002 United States House of Representatives elections in Indiana</a></div>

<p>The state lost one seat in reapportionment.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Oklahoma">Oklahoma</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2002_United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Oklahoma">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
